Episode List

This list contains every film and television episode I own on physical media. I have neither cable television nor a subscription to a streaming service, but I do have over six years of normal viewing here.

Idiosyncratic, and often arbitrary, decisions abound here. I categorised films the way I felt like. Sorting by episode names ignores articles, as you might expect, but also ignores most anything that would otherwise result in too large a batch of the same series appearing together. For instance, check episodes of Scrubs or Day Break, or Simpsons episodes with character names in the title.

Remove Series Name

For a sortable list of episodes, please enable JavaScript or check out the JSON object here.

The round buttons on the left-hand sidebottom of the screen can be used to sort the episodes in four different ways.

  • R: Random – Shuffles the list. Press again to get a new viewing order.
  • A: Airdate – Sorts by the date of the original broadcast or release.
  • T: Title – Sorts by film title or TV episode name, ignoring articles.
  • L: Title length – Sorts by the length of the full title.
  • C: Calendar Date – Sorts by the day of the year the episode first aired.
  • D: Default sort – Groups TV series set in the same universe together.
